(** Characterization of opcartesian 2-cells *)

C₁, C₂: bicat_of_univ_cats
F₁, F₂: bicat_of_univ_cats ⟦ C₁, C₂ ⟧
α: F₁ ==> F₂
D₁: disp_bicat_of_opcleaving C₁
D₂: disp_bicat_of_opcleaving C₂
FF₁: D₁ -->[ F₁] D₂
FF₂: D₁ -->[ F₂] D₂
αα: FF₁ ==>[ α] FF₂
Hαα: ∏ (x : C₁ : univalent_category)
(xx : (pr1 D₁ : disp_univalent_category C₁) x),
is_opcartesian ((pr11 αα) x xx)
is_opcartesian_2cell disp_bicat_of_opcleaving αα

isaprop (∑ γγ : FF₂ ==>[ β] GG, αα •• γγ = βα)
 abstract
      (use invproofirrelevance ;
       intros φ₁ φ₂ ;
       use subtypePath ; [ intro ; apply disp_cellset_property | ] ;
       use subtypePath ; [ intro ; apply isapropunit | ] ;
       use disp_nat_trans_eq ;
       intros x xx ;
       assert (p₁ := maponpaths (λ z, (pr11 z) x xx) (pr2 φ₁)) ;
       assert (p₂ := maponpaths (λ z, (pr11 z) x xx) (pr2 φ₂)) ;
       cbn in p₁, p₂ ;
       pose (r := p₁ @ !p₂) ;
       use (opcartesian_factorisation_unique (Hαα x xx)) ;
       exact r).

 exact (opcartesian_factorisation_disp_nat_trans (pr1 αα) (pr1 βα) Hαα).
    
C₁, C₂: bicat_of_univ_cats

  (opcartesian_factorisation_disp_nat_trans (pr1 αα)
     (pr1 βα) Hαα,, tt)
 abstract
        (use subtypePath ; [ intro ; apply isapropunit | ] ;
         use subtypePath ; [ intro ; apply isaprop_disp_nat_trans_axioms| ] ;
         use funextsec ; intro x ;
         use funextsec ; intro xx ;
         apply opcartesian_factorisation_commutes).
Defined.

(** Characterization of cartesian 2-cells *)
Section OpCleavingOfOpCleavingPointwiseCartesian.
  Context {C₁ C₂ : bicat_of_univ_cats}
          {F₁ F₂ : C₁ --> C₂}
          {α : F₁ ==> F₂}
          {D₁ : disp_bicat_of_opcleaving C₁}
          {D₂ : disp_bicat_of_opcleaving C₂}
          {FF₁ : D₁ -->[ F₁ ] D₂}
          {FF₂ : D₁ -->[ F₂ ] D₂}
          (αα : FF₁ ==>[ α ] FF₂)
          (Hαα : is_opcartesian_2cell disp_bicat_of_opcleaving αα).

  Let lift_FF₂
    : disp_functor F₂ (pr11 D₁) (pr11 D₂)
    := opcartesian_factorisation_disp_functor
         (pr2 D₂)
         (pr1 FF₁)
         α.

  (pr2 D₂) (pr1 FF₁) α: disp_functor F₂ (pr11 D₁) (pr11 D₂)
D₁ -->[ F₂] D₂

    apply (pr2 FF₁).
  Defined.

  Definition pointwise_opcartesian_lift_data
    : disp_nat_trans_data
        (pr1 α)
        (pr11 FF₁)
        lift_FF₂
    := λ x xx, opcleaving_mor (pr2 D₂) (pr1 α x) (pr11 FF₁ x xx).

  (pr2 D₂) (pr1 FF₁) α

(♯ (pr11 FF₁) ff ;; pointwise_opcartesian_lift_data y
                      yy)%mor_disp =

  (mor_disp ((pr11 FF₁) x xx) (lift_FF₂ y yy))
  (nat_trans_ax α x y f)
  (pointwise_opcartesian_lift_data x xx ;; ♯ lift_FF₂
                                             ff)%mor_disp

lift_FF₂:= opcartesian_factorisation_disp_functor
  (pr2 D₂) (pr1 FF₁) α: disp_functor F₂ (pr11 D₁) (pr11 D₂)
lift_FF₂_opfib:= lift_FF₂,,
opcartesian_factorisation_disp_functor_is_opcartesian
  (pr2 D₂) (pr1 FF₁) α 
  (pr2 FF₁): D₁ -->[ F₂] D₂
x: C₁ : univalent_category
xx: (pr1 D₁ : disp_univalent_category C₁) x
p:= maponpaths
  (λ z : ∑
         _ : disp_nat_trans α (pr1 FF₁) (pr1 FF₂),
         unit, (pr11 z) x xx)
  (is_opcartesian_2cell_unique_iso_com Hαα
     pointwise_opcartesian_lift_data_is_opcartesian): (pr11 αα) x xx =
(pr11 (transportf
         (λ z : F₁ ⟹ F₂,
          ∑
          _ : disp_nat_trans z (pr1 FF₁) (pr1 FF₂),
          unit) (id2_right α)
         (disp_nat_trans_comp
            pointwise_opcartesian_lift
            (opcartesian_factorisation_disp_nat_trans
               pointwise_opcartesian_lift
               (pr1
                  (transportb
                     (λ 
                      z : F₁ ⟹ F₂,
                      ∑
                      _ : 
                      disp_nat_trans z 
                      (pr1 FF₁) 
                      (pr1 FF₂), unit)
                     (id2_right α) αα))
               pointwise_opcartesian_lift_data_pointwise_opcartesian),,
          tt))) x xx
(pr11 αα) x xx =
transportf
  (λ z : C₂ ⟦ F₁ x, F₂ x ⟧,
   (pr11 FF₁) x xx -->[ z] pr1 FF₂ x xx)
  (nat_trans_eq_pointwise (id2_right α) x)
  (pointwise_opcartesian_lift_data x xx ;; opcartesian_factorisation_disp_nat_trans_data
                                             pointwise_opcartesian_lift
                                             (pr1
                                                (transportb
                                                 (λ 
                                                 z : 
                                                 F₁

                                                 ∑
                                                 _ : 
                                                 disp_nat_trans
                                                 z
                                                 (pr11 FF₁)
                                                 (pr11 FF₂),
                                                 unit)
                                                 (id2_right
                                                 α) αα))
                                             pointwise_opcartesian_lift_data_pointwise_opcartesian
                                             x xx)%mor_disp

      exact (p @ (@disp_nat_trans_transportf _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _)).

  (?pr1,, tt)

D₁: ∑ d : disp_univalent_category C₁,
opcleaving (pr1 d)
D₂: ∑ d : disp_univalent_category C₂,
opcleaving (pr1 d)
F, G: C₁ ⟶ C₂
FF: ∑ fD : disp_functor F (pr1 D₁) (pr1 D₂),
is_opcartesian_disp_functor fD
α: F ⟹ G
disp_nat_trans α (pr1 FF)
  (opcartesian_factorisation_disp_functor_data
     (pr2 D₂) (pr1 FF) α)
 exact (opcartesian_factorisation_disp_functor_cell (pr2 D₂) (pr1 FF) α).
    
C₁, C₂: univalent_category
D₁: ∑ d : disp_univalent_category C₁,
opcleaving (pr1 d)
D₂: ∑ d : disp_univalent_category C₂,
opcleaving (pr1 d)
F, G: C₁ ⟶ C₂
FF: ∑ fD : disp_functor F (pr1 D₁) (pr1 D₂),
is_opcartesian_disp_functor fD
α: F ⟹ G
(λ αα : ∑
        _ : disp_nat_trans α (pr1 FF)
              (opcartesian_factorisation_disp_functor_data
                 (pr2 D₂) (pr1 FF) α), unit,
 is_opcartesian_2cell disp_bicat_of_opcleaving αα)
  (opcartesian_factorisation_disp_functor_cell
     (pr2 D₂) (pr1 FF) α,, tt)
 
C₁, C₂: univalent_category
D₁: ∑ d : disp_univalent_category C₁,
opcleaving (pr1 d)
D₂: ∑ d : disp_univalent_category C₂,
opcleaving (pr1 d)
F, G: C₁ ⟶ C₂
FF: ∑ fD : disp_functor F (pr1 D₁) (pr1 D₂),
is_opcartesian_disp_functor fD
α: F ⟹ G
∏ (x : C₁) (xx : pr1 D₁ x),
is_opcartesian
  ((pr11 (opcartesian_factorisation_disp_functor_cell
            (pr2 D₂) (pr1 FF) α,, tt)) x xx)

      apply opcartesian_factorisation_disp_functor_cell_is_opcartesian.
Defined.

          (pr2 HH)) ;; cleaving_of_opcleaving_lift_mor

       id2_invertible_2cell (H · F)] HH,
 is_disp_invertible_2cell
   (id2_invertible_2cell (H · F)) x) (?pr1,, tt)

yy: pr1 D₃ y
ff: xx -->[ f] yy

  (maponpaths (compose (# F (# H₁ f)))
     (cleaving_of_opcleaving_lift_2cell_data_subproof
        y) @ ! functor_comp F (# H₁ f) (α y))
  (♯ (pr11 Lh) ff ;; ((pr111 (pr2 Lh)) y yy ;; (pr11 αα)
                                                 y yy ;; 
                      (pr111 (pr22 Lh')) y yy))%mor_disp =

     (mor_disp ((pr11 Lh) x xx) ((pr11 Lh') y yy))
     (cancel_postcomposition
        (id₁ (F (H₁ x)) · # (pr1 F) (pr1 α x)
         · id₁ (F (H₂ x))) (# F (α x)) (# F (# H₂ f))

     ((pr111 (pr2 Lh)) x xx ;; (pr11 αα) x xx ;; (pr111 
                                                 (pr22 Lh'))
                                                 x xx ;; 
      ♯ (pr11 Lh') ff)%mor_disp)

  (mor_disp ((pr11 Lh) x xx) ((pr11 Lh') y yy))
  (assoc (id₁ (F (H₁ x))) (# F (# H₁ f))
     (# (pr1 F) (pr1 α y) · id₁ (F (H₂ y))) @
   assoc (id₁ (F (H₁ x)) · # F (# H₁ f))
     (# (pr1 F) (pr1 α y)) (id₁ (F (H₂ y))) @
   cancel_postcomposition
     (id₁ (F (H₁ x)) · # F (# H₁ f)
      · # (pr1 F) (pr1 α y))
     (# F (# H₁ f) · id₁ (F (H₁ y))
      · # (pr1 F) (pr1 α y)) (id₁ (F (H₂ y)))
     (cancel_postcomposition
        (id₁ (F (H₁ x)) · # F (# H₁ f))

        (# (pr1 F) (pr1 α y))
        (! is_nat_trans_id
             (functor_composite_data H₁ F) x y f)) @
   cancel_postcomposition
     (# F (# H₁ f) · id₁ (F (H₁ y))
      · # (pr1 F) (pr1 α y))
     (# F (# H₁ f)
      · (id₁ (F (H₁ y)) · # (pr1 F) (pr1 α y)))
     (id₁ (F (H₂ y)))
     (! assoc (# F (# H₁ f)) (id₁ (F (H₁ y)))
          (# (pr1 F) (pr1 α y))) @
   ! assoc (# F (# H₁ f))
       (id₁ (F (H₁ y)) · # (pr1 F) (pr1 α y))
       (id₁ (F (H₂ y))) @
   maponpaths (compose (# F (# H₁ f)))

  (assoc ((α ▹ F) x) (# (H₂ · F) f) (id₁ (F (H₂ y))) @
   cancel_postcomposition ((α ▹ F) x · # (H₂ · F) f)
     (# F (# H₁ f) · # (pr1 F) (pr1 α y))
     (id₁ (F (H₂ y))) (! nat_trans_ax (α ▹ F) x y f) @
   ! assoc (# F (# H₁ f)) (# (pr1 F) (pr1 α y))

       (id₁ (F (H₂ y))) @

D₂: disp_bicat_of_opcleaving C₂
D₃: disp_bicat_of_opcleaving C₃
HH₁: D₃ -->[ H₁ · F] D₂
HH₂: D₃ -->[ H₂ · F] D₂
αα: HH₁ ==>[ α ▹ F] HH₂
Lh: lift_1cell_factor disp_bicat_of_opcleaving
  (cleaving_of_opcleaving_lift_mor D₂ F) HH₁
Lh': lift_1cell_factor disp_bicat_of_opcleaving
(cleaving_of_opcleaving_lift_mor D₂ F) HH₂
x, y: C₃
f: C₃ ⟦ x, y ⟧
xx: pr1 D₃ x
yy: pr1 D₃ y
ff: xx -->[ f] yy
transportf
  (mor_disp ((pr11 Lh) x xx) ((pr11 Lh') y yy))
  (maponpaths (compose (id₁ (F (H₁ x))))
     (assoc ((α ▹ F) x) (# (H₂ · F) f)
        (id₁ (F (H₂ y))) @
      cancel_postcomposition
        ((α ▹ F) x · # (H₂ · F) f)
        (# F (# H₁ f) · # (pr1 F) (pr1 α y))
        (id₁ (F (H₂ y)))
        (! nat_trans_ax (α ▹ F) x y f) @
      ! assoc (# F (# H₁ f)) (# (pr1 F) (pr1 α y))
          (id₁ (F (H₂ y)))) @
   assoc (id₁ (F (H₁ x))) (# F (# H₁ f))
     (# (pr1 F) (pr1 α y) · id₁ (F (H₂ y))) @
   assoc (id₁ (F (H₁ x)) · # F (# H₁ f))
     (# (pr1 F) (pr1 α y)) (id₁ (F (H₂ y))) @
   cancel_postcomposition
     (id₁ (F (H₁ x)) · # F (# H₁ f)
      · # (pr1 F) (pr1 α y))
     (# F (# H₁ f) · id₁ (F (H₁ y))
      · # (pr1 F) (pr1 α y)) (id₁ (F (H₂ y)))
     (cancel_postcomposition
        (id₁ (F (H₁ x)) · # F (# H₁ f))
        (# F (# H₁ f) · id₁ (F (H₁ y)))
        (# (pr1 F) (pr1 α y))
        (! is_nat_trans_id
             (functor_composite_data H₁ F) x y f)) @
   cancel_postcomposition
     (# F (# H₁ f) · id₁ (F (H₁ y))
      · # (pr1 F) (pr1 α y))
     (# F (# H₁ f)
      · (id₁ (F (H₁ y)) · # (pr1 F) (pr1 α y)))
     (id₁ (F (H₂ y)))
     (! assoc (# F (# H₁ f)) (id₁ (F (H₁ y)))
          (# (pr1 F) (pr1 α y))) @
   ! assoc (# F (# H₁ f))
       (id₁ (F (H₁ y)) · # (pr1 F) (pr1 α y))
       (id₁ (F (H₂ y))) @
   maponpaths (compose (# F (# H₁ f)))
     (cleaving_of_opcleaving_lift_2cell_data_subproof
        y) @ ! functor_comp F (# H₁ f) (α y))
  (transportf
     (mor_disp ((pr11 Lh) x xx)
        (pr1
           (pr1 Lh' ;; cleaving_of_opcleaving_lift_mor
                         D₂ F)%mor_disp y yy))
     (maponpaths (compose (id₁ (F (H₁ x))))
        (maponpaths (compose ((α ▹ F) x))
           (! nat_trans_ax
                (id2_invertible_2cell (H₂ · F)) ^-1 x
                y f)))
     ((pr112 Lh) x xx ;; (pr1 αα x xx ;; ((pr112 (pr2
                                                 Lh'))
                                            x xx ;; 
                                          ♯ (pr1
                                               (pr1
                                                 Lh' ;; 
                                                cleaving_of_opcleaving_lift_mor
                                                 D₂ F))
                                            ff)))%mor_disp) =
transportf
  (mor_disp ((pr11 Lh) x xx) ((pr11 Lh') y yy))
  (! nat_trans_ax α x y f)
  (transportf
     (mor_disp ((pr11 Lh) x xx) ((pr11 Lh') y yy))
     (cancel_postcomposition
        (id₁ (F (H₁ x)) · # (pr1 F) (pr1 α x)
         · id₁ (F (H₂ x))) (# F (α x)) (# F (# H₂ f))
        (cleaving_of_opcleaving_lift_2cell_data_subproof
           x) @ ! functor_comp F (α x) (# H₂ f))
     ((pr111 (pr2 Lh)) x xx ;; (pr11 αα) x xx ;; (pr111 
                                                 (pr22 Lh'))
                                                 x xx ;; 
      ♯ (pr11 Lh') ff)%mor_disp)

C₁, C₂, C₃: bicat_of_univ_cats
F: bicat_of_univ_cats ⟦ C₁, C₂ ⟧
H₁, H₂: bicat_of_univ_cats ⟦ C₃, C₁ ⟧
α: H₁ ==> H₂

?b =
transportf
  (mor_disp ((pr11 Lh) x xx) ((pr11 Lh') y yy))
  (maponpaths (compose (id₁ (F (H₁ x))))
     (maponpaths (compose (# (pr1 F) (pr1 α x)))
        (! is_nat_trans_id
             (functor_composite_data H₂ F) x y f)) @
   maponpaths (compose (id₁ (F (H₁ x))))
     (assoc (# (pr1 F) (pr1 α x)) (# F (# H₂ f))
        (id₁ (F (H₂ y))) @
      cancel_postcomposition
        (# (pr1 F) (pr1 α x) · # F (# H₂ f))
        (# F (# H₁ f) · # (pr1 F) (pr1 α y))
        (id₁ (F (H₂ y)))
        (! is_nat_trans_post_whisker C₃ C₁ C₂ H₁ H₂ α
             F x y f) @
      ! assoc (# F (# H₁ f)) (# (pr1 F) (pr1 α y))
          (id₁ (F (H₂ y)))) @
   assoc (id₁ (F (H₁ x))) (# F (# H₁ f))
     (# (pr1 F) (pr1 α y) · id₁ (F (H₂ y))) @
   assoc (id₁ (F (H₁ x)) · # F (# H₁ f))
     (# (pr1 F) (pr1 α y)) (id₁ (F (H₂ y))) @
   cancel_postcomposition
     (id₁ (F (H₁ x)) · # F (# H₁ f)
      · # (pr1 F) (pr1 α y))
     (# F (# H₁ f) · id₁ (F (H₁ y))
      · # (pr1 F) (pr1 α y)) (id₁ (F (H₂ y)))
     (cancel_postcomposition
        (id₁ (F (H₁ x)) · # F (# H₁ f))
        (# F (# H₁ f) · id₁ (F (H₁ y)))
        (# (pr1 F) (pr1 α y))
        (! is_nat_trans_id
             (functor_composite_data H₁ F) x y f)) @
   cancel_postcomposition
     (# F (# H₁ f) · id₁ (F (H₁ y))
      · # (pr1 F) (pr1 α y))
     (# F (# H₁ f)
      · (id₁ (F (H₁ y)) · # (pr1 F) (pr1 α y)))
     (id₁ (F (H₂ y)))
     (! assoc (# F (# H₁ f)) (id₁ (F (H₁ y)))
          (# (pr1 F) (pr1 α y))) @
   ! assoc (# F (# H₁ f))
       (id₁ (F (H₁ y)) · # (pr1 F) (pr1 α y))
       (id₁ (F (H₂ y))) @
   maponpaths (compose (# F (# H₁ f)))
     (cleaving_of_opcleaving_lift_2cell_data_subproof
        y) @ ! functor_comp F (# H₁ f) (α y))
  ((pr112 Lh) x xx ;; (pr1 αα x xx ;; ((pr112 (pr2 Lh'))
                                         x xx ;; ♯ (pr11 Lh')
                                                 ff)))%mor_disp

HH₂: D₃ -->[ H₂ · F] D₂
αα: HH₁ ==>[ α ▹ F] HH₂

(cleaving_of_opcleaving_lift_mor D₂ F) HH₂
x, y: C₃
f: C₃ ⟦ x, y ⟧
xx: pr1 D₃ x
yy: pr1 D₃ y
ff: xx -->[ f] yy
transportf
  (mor_disp ((pr11 Lh) x xx) ((pr11 Lh') y yy))
  (! nat_trans_ax α x y f)
  (transportf
     (mor_disp ((pr11 Lh) x xx) ((pr11 Lh') y yy))
     (cancel_postcomposition
        (id₁ (F (H₁ x)) · # (pr1 F) (pr1 α x)
         · id₁ (F (H₂ x))) (# F (α x)) (# F (# H₂ f))
        (cleaving_of_opcleaving_lift_2cell_data_subproof
           x) @ ! functor_comp F (α x) (# H₂ f))
     ((pr111 (pr2 Lh)) x xx ;; (pr11 αα) x xx ;; (pr111 
                                                 (pr22 Lh'))
                                                 x xx ;; 
      ♯ (pr11 Lh') ff)%mor_disp) = ?b

      apply transportf_reindex.
    
C₁, C₂, C₃: bicat_of_univ_cats
F: bicat_of_univ_cats ⟦ C₁, C₂ ⟧
H₁, H₂: bicat_of_univ_cats ⟦ C₃, C₁ ⟧
α: H₁ ==> H₂
D₂: disp_bicat_of_opcleaving C₂
D₃: disp_bicat_of_opcleaving C₃
HH₁: D₃ -->[ H₁ · F] D₂
HH₂: D₃ -->[ H₂ · F] D₂
αα: HH₁ ==>[ α ▹ F] HH₂
Lh: lift_1cell_factor disp_bicat_of_opcleaving
  (cleaving_of_opcleaving_lift_mor D₂ F) HH₁
Lh': lift_1cell_factor disp_bicat_of_opcleaving
(cleaving_of_opcleaving_lift_mor D₂ F) HH₂
x, y: C₃
f: C₃ ⟦ x, y ⟧
xx: pr1 D₃ x
yy: pr1 D₃ y
ff: xx -->[ f] yy
transportf
  (mor_disp ((pr11 Lh) x xx) ((pr11 Lh') y yy))
  (maponpaths # F (! nat_trans_ax α x y f))
  (transportf
     (mor_disp ((pr11 Lh) x xx) ((pr11 Lh') y yy))
     (cancel_postcomposition
        (id₁ (F (H₁ x)) · # (pr1 F) (pr1 α x)
         · id₁ (F (H₂ x))) (# F (α x)) (# F (# H₂ f))
        (cleaving_of_opcleaving_lift_2cell_data_subproof
           x) @ ! functor_comp F (α x) (# H₂ f))
     ((pr111 (pr2 Lh)) x xx ;; (pr11 αα) x xx ;; (pr111 
                                                 (pr22 Lh'))
                                                 x xx ;; 
      ♯ (pr11 Lh') ff)%mor_disp) =
transportf
  (mor_disp ((pr11 Lh) x xx) ((pr11 Lh') y yy))
  (maponpaths (compose (id₁ (F (H₁ x))))
     (maponpaths (compose (# (pr1 F) (pr1 α x)))
        (! is_nat_trans_id
             (functor_composite_data H₂ F) x y f)) @
   maponpaths (compose (id₁ (F (H₁ x))))
     (assoc (# (pr1 F) (pr1 α x)) (# F (# H₂ f))
        (id₁ (F (H₂ y))) @
      cancel_postcomposition
        (# (pr1 F) (pr1 α x) · # F (# H₂ f))
        (# F (# H₁ f) · # (pr1 F) (pr1 α y))
        (id₁ (F (H₂ y)))
        (! is_nat_trans_post_whisker C₃ C₁ C₂ H₁ H₂ α
             F x y f) @
      ! assoc (# F (# H₁ f)) (# (pr1 F) (pr1 α y))
          (id₁ (F (H₂ y)))) @
   assoc (id₁ (F (H₁ x))) (# F (# H₁ f))
     (# (pr1 F) (pr1 α y) · id₁ (F (H₂ y))) @
   assoc (id₁ (F (H₁ x)) · # F (# H₁ f))
     (# (pr1 F) (pr1 α y)) (id₁ (F (H₂ y))) @
   cancel_postcomposition
     (id₁ (F (H₁ x)) · # F (# H₁ f)
      · # (pr1 F) (pr1 α y))
     (# F (# H₁ f) · id₁ (F (H₁ y))
      · # (pr1 F) (pr1 α y)) (id₁ (F (H₂ y)))
     (cancel_postcomposition
        (id₁ (F (H₁ x)) · # F (# H₁ f))
        (# F (# H₁ f) · id₁ (F (H₁ y)))
        (# (pr1 F) (pr1 α y))
        (! is_nat_trans_id
             (functor_composite_data H₁ F) x y f)) @
   cancel_postcomposition
     (# F (# H₁ f) · id₁ (F (H₁ y))
      · # (pr1 F) (pr1 α y))
     (# F (# H₁ f)
      · (id₁ (F (H₁ y)) · # (pr1 F) (pr1 α y)))
     (id₁ (F (H₂ y)))
     (! assoc (# F (# H₁ f)) (id₁ (F (H₁ y)))
          (# (pr1 F) (pr1 α y))) @
   ! assoc (# F (# H₁ f))
       (id₁ (F (H₁ y)) · # (pr1 F) (pr1 α y))
       (id₁ (F (H₂ y))) @
   maponpaths (compose (# F (# H₁ f)))
     (cleaving_of_opcleaving_lift_2cell_data_subproof
        y) @ ! functor_comp F (# H₁ f) (α y))
  ((pr112 Lh) x xx ;; (pr1 αα x xx ;; ((pr112 (pr2 Lh'))
                                         x xx ;; ♯ (pr11 Lh')
                                                 ff)))%mor_disp

  (mor_disp ((pr11 Lh) x xx) ((pr11 Lh') y yy))
  ((cancel_postcomposition
      (id₁ (F (H₁ x)) · # (pr1 F) (pr1 α x)
       · id₁ (F (H₂ x))) (# F (α x)) (# F (# H₂ f))
      (cleaving_of_opcleaving_lift_2cell_data_subproof
         x) @ ! functor_comp F (α x) (# H₂ f)) @
   maponpaths # F (! nat_trans_ax α x y f))
  ((pr111 (pr2 Lh)) x xx ;; (pr11 αα) x xx ;; (pr111 
                                               (pr22 Lh'))
                                                x xx ;; 
   ♯ (pr11 Lh') ff)%mor_disp

    
C₁, C₂, C₃: bicat_of_univ_cats
F: bicat_of_univ_cats ⟦ C₁, C₂ ⟧
H₁, H₂: bicat_of_univ_cats ⟦ C₃, C₁ ⟧
α: H₁ ==> H₂
D₂: disp_bicat_of_opcleaving C₂
D₃: disp_bicat_of_opcleaving C₃
HH₁: D₃ -->[ H₁ · F] D₂
HH₂: D₃ -->[ H₂ · F] D₂
αα: HH₁ ==>[ α ▹ F] HH₂
Lh: lift_1cell_factor disp_bicat_of_opcleaving
  (cleaving_of_opcleaving_lift_mor D₂ F) HH₁
Lh': lift_1cell_factor disp_bicat_of_opcleaving
(cleaving_of_opcleaving_lift_mor D₂ F) HH₂
x, y: C₃
f: C₃ ⟦ x, y ⟧
xx: pr1 D₃ x
yy: pr1 D₃ y
ff: xx -->[ f] yy
transportf
  (mor_disp ((pr11 Lh) x xx) ((pr11 Lh') y yy))
  (! assoc (id₁ (F (H₁ x)) · # (pr1 F) (pr1 α x))
       (id₁ (F (H₂ x))) (# F (# H₂ f)) @
   ! assoc (id₁ (F (H₁ x))) (# (pr1 F) (pr1 α x))
       (id₁ (F (H₂ x)) · # F (# H₂ f)) @
   maponpaths (compose (id₁ (F (H₁ x))))
     (maponpaths (compose (# (pr1 F) (pr1 α x)))
        (! is_nat_trans_id
             (functor_composite_data H₂ F) x y f)) @
   maponpaths (compose (id₁ (F (H₁ x))))
     (assoc (# (pr1 F) (pr1 α x)) (# F (# H₂ f))
        (id₁ (F (H₂ y))) @
      cancel_postcomposition
        (# (pr1 F) (pr1 α x) · # F (# H₂ f))
        (# F (# H₁ f) · # (pr1 F) (pr1 α y))
        (id₁ (F (H₂ y)))
        (! is_nat_trans_post_whisker C₃ C₁ C₂ H₁ H₂ α
             F x y f) @
      ! assoc (# F (# H₁ f)) (# (pr1 F) (pr1 α y))
          (id₁ (F (H₂ y)))) @
   assoc (id₁ (F (H₁ x))) (# F (# H₁ f))
     (# (pr1 F) (pr1 α y) · id₁ (F (H₂ y))) @
   assoc (id₁ (F (H₁ x)) · # F (# H₁ f))
     (# (pr1 F) (pr1 α y)) (id₁ (F (H₂ y))) @
   cancel_postcomposition
     (id₁ (F (H₁ x)) · # F (# H₁ f)
      · # (pr1 F) (pr1 α y))
     (# F (# H₁ f) · id₁ (F (H₁ y))
      · # (pr1 F) (pr1 α y)) (id₁ (F (H₂ y)))
     (cancel_postcomposition
        (id₁ (F (H₁ x)) · # F (# H₁ f))
        (# F (# H₁ f) · id₁ (F (H₁ y)))
        (# (pr1 F) (pr1 α y))
        (! is_nat_trans_id
             (functor_composite_data H₁ F) x y f)) @
   cancel_postcomposition
     (# F (# H₁ f) · id₁ (F (H₁ y))
      · # (pr1 F) (pr1 α y))
     (# F (# H₁ f)
      · (id₁ (F (H₁ y)) · # (pr1 F) (pr1 α y)))
     (id₁ (F (H₂ y)))
     (! assoc (# F (# H₁ f)) (id₁ (F (H₁ y)))
          (# (pr1 F) (pr1 α y))) @
   ! assoc (# F (# H₁ f))
       (id₁ (F (H₁ y)) · # (pr1 F) (pr1 α y))
       (id₁ (F (H₂ y))) @
   maponpaths (compose (# F (# H₁ f)))
     (cleaving_of_opcleaving_lift_2cell_data_subproof
        y) @ ! functor_comp F (# H₁ f) (α y))
  ((pr112 Lh) x xx ;; pr1 αα x xx ;; (pr112 (pr2 Lh'))
                                       x xx ;; ♯ (pr11 Lh')
                                                 ff)%mor_disp =
transportf
  (mor_disp ((pr11 Lh) x xx) ((pr11 Lh') y yy))
  ((cancel_postcomposition
      (id₁ (F (H₁ x)) · # (pr1 F) (pr1 α x)
       · id₁ (F (H₂ x))) (# F (α x)) (# F (# H₂ f))
      (cleaving_of_opcleaving_lift_2cell_data_subproof
         x) @ ! functor_comp F (α x) (# H₂ f)) @
   maponpaths # F (! nat_trans_ax α x y f))
  ((pr111 (pr2 Lh)) x xx ;; (pr11 αα) x xx ;; (pr111 
                                               (pr22 Lh'))
                                                x xx ;;

C₁, C₂, C₃: bicat_of_univ_cats
F: bicat_of_univ_cats ⟦ C₁, C₂ ⟧
H₁, H₂: bicat_of_univ_cats ⟦ C₃, C₁ ⟧
α: H₁ ==> H₂
D₂: disp_bicat_of_opcleaving C₂
D₃: disp_bicat_of_opcleaving C₃

αα: HH₁ ==>[ α ▹ F] HH₂

  (cleaving_of_opcleaving_lift_mor D₂ F) HH₁
Lh': lift_1cell_factor disp_bicat_of_opcleaving
(cleaving_of_opcleaving_lift_mor D₂ F) HH₂
x, y: C₃
f: C₃ ⟦ x, y ⟧
xx: pr1 D₃ x
yy: pr1 D₃ y
ff: xx -->[ f] yy
! assoc (id₁ (F (H₁ x)) · # (pr1 F) (pr1 α x))
    (id₁ (F (H₂ x))) (# F (# H₂ f)) @
! assoc (id₁ (F (H₁ x))) (# (pr1 F) (pr1 α x))
    (id₁ (F (H₂ x)) · # F (# H₂ f)) @
maponpaths (compose (id₁ (F (H₁ x))))
  (maponpaths (compose (# (pr1 F) (pr1 α x)))
     (! is_nat_trans_id (functor_composite_data H₂ F)
          x y f)) @
maponpaths (compose (id₁ (F (H₁ x))))
  (assoc (# (pr1 F) (pr1 α x)) (# F (# H₂ f))
     (id₁ (F (H₂ y))) @
   cancel_postcomposition
     (# (pr1 F) (pr1 α x) · # F (# H₂ f))
     (# F (# H₁ f) · # (pr1 F) (pr1 α y))
     (id₁ (F (H₂ y)))
     (! is_nat_trans_post_whisker C₃ C₁ C₂ H₁ H₂ α F x
          y f) @
   ! assoc (# F (# H₁ f)) (# (pr1 F) (pr1 α y))
       (id₁ (F (H₂ y)))) @
assoc (id₁ (F (H₁ x))) (# F (# H₁ f))
  (# (pr1 F) (pr1 α y) · id₁ (F (H₂ y))) @
assoc (id₁ (F (H₁ x)) · # F (# H₁ f))
  (# (pr1 F) (pr1 α y)) (id₁ (F (H₂ y))) @
cancel_postcomposition
  (id₁ (F (H₁ x)) · # F (# H₁ f) · # (pr1 F) (pr1 α y))
  (# F (# H₁ f) · id₁ (F (H₁ y)) · # (pr1 F) (pr1 α y))
  (id₁ (F (H₂ y)))
  (cancel_postcomposition
     (id₁ (F (H₁ x)) · # F (# H₁ f))
     (# F (# H₁ f) · id₁ (F (H₁ y)))
     (# (pr1 F) (pr1 α y))
     (! is_nat_trans_id (functor_composite_data H₁ F)
          x y f)) @
cancel_postcomposition
  (# F (# H₁ f) · id₁ (F (H₁ y)) · # (pr1 F) (pr1 α y))
  (# F (# H₁ f)
   · (id₁ (F (H₁ y)) · # (pr1 F) (pr1 α y)))
  (id₁ (F (H₂ y)))
  (! assoc (# F (# H₁ f)) (id₁ (F (H₁ y)))
       (# (pr1 F) (pr1 α y))) @
! assoc (# F (# H₁ f))
    (id₁ (F (H₁ y)) · # (pr1 F) (pr1 α y))
    (id₁ (F (H₂ y))) @
maponpaths (compose (# F (# H₁ f)))
  (cleaving_of_opcleaving_lift_2cell_data_subproof y) @
! functor_comp F (# H₁ f) (α y) =
(cancel_postcomposition
   (id₁ (F (H₁ x)) · # (pr1 F) (pr1 α x)
    · id₁ (F (H₂ x))) (# F (α x)) (# F (# H₂ f))
   (cleaving_of_opcleaving_lift_2cell_data_subproof x) @
 ! functor_comp F (α x) (# H₂ f)) @
maponpaths # F (! nat_trans_ax α x y f)

    apply homset_property.
  Qed.

Lh: lift_1cell_factor disp_bicat_of_opcleaving
  (cleaving_of_opcleaving_lift_mor D₂ F) HH₁
Lh': lift_1cell_factor disp_bicat_of_opcleaving
(cleaving_of_opcleaving_lift_mor D₂ F) HH₂
(λ δδ : Lh ==>[ α] Lh',
 transportf
   (λ z : H₁ · F ==> H₂ · F,
    Lh ;; cleaving_of_opcleaving_lift_mor D₂ F ==>[
    z] HH₂) (id2_right (α ▹ F) @ ! id2_left (α ▹ F))
   ((δδ ▹▹ cleaving_of_opcleaving_lift_mor D₂ F)
    •• disp_cell_lift_1cell_factor
         disp_bicat_of_opcleaving
         (cleaving_of_opcleaving_lift_mor D₂ F) Lh') =
 disp_cell_lift_1cell_factor disp_bicat_of_opcleaving
   (cleaving_of_opcleaving_lift_mor D₂ F) Lh •• αα)
  (?pr1,, tt)

      
C₁, C₂, C₃: bicat_of_univ_cats
F: bicat_of_univ_cats ⟦ C₁, C₂ ⟧
H₁, H₂: bicat_of_univ_cats ⟦ C₃, C₁ ⟧
α: H₁ ==> H₂
D₂: disp_bicat_of_opcleaving C₂
D₃: disp_bicat_of_opcleaving C₃
HH₁: D₃ -->[ H₁ · F] D₂
HH₂: D₃ -->[ H₂ · F] D₂
αα: HH₁ ==>[ α ▹ F] HH₂
Lh: lift_1cell_factor disp_bicat_of_opcleaving
  (cleaving_of_opcleaving_lift_mor D₂ F) HH₁
Lh': lift_1cell_factor disp_bicat_of_opcleaving
(cleaving_of_opcleaving_lift_mor D₂ F) HH₂
pr1 Lh ==>[ α] pr1 Lh'
 exact cleaving_of_opcleaving_lift_2cell.
      
C₁, C₂, C₃: bicat_of_univ_cats
F: bicat_of_univ_cats ⟦ C₁, C₂ ⟧
H₁, H₂: bicat_of_univ_cats ⟦ C₃, C₁ ⟧
α: H₁ ==> H₂
D₂: disp_bicat_of_opcleaving C₂
D₃: disp_bicat_of_opcleaving C₃
HH₁: D₃ -->[ H₁ · F] D₂
HH₂: D₃ -->[ H₂ · F] D₂
αα: HH₁ ==>[ α ▹ F] HH₂
Lh: lift_1cell_factor disp_bicat_of_opcleaving
  (cleaving_of_opcleaving_lift_mor D₂ F) HH₁
Lh': lift_1cell_factor disp_bicat_of_opcleaving
(cleaving_of_opcleaving_lift_mor D₂ F) HH₂
(λ δδ : Lh ==>[ α] Lh',
 transportf
   (λ z : H₁ · F ==> H₂ · F,
    Lh ;; cleaving_of_opcleaving_lift_mor D₂ F ==>[
    z] HH₂) (id2_right (α ▹ F) @ ! id2_left (α ▹ F))
   ((δδ ▹▹ cleaving_of_opcleaving_lift_mor D₂ F)
    •• disp_cell_lift_1cell_factor
         disp_bicat_of_opcleaving
         (cleaving_of_opcleaving_lift_mor D₂ F) Lh') =
 disp_cell_lift_1cell_factor disp_bicat_of_opcleaving
   (cleaving_of_opcleaving_lift_mor D₂ F) Lh •• αα)
  (cleaving_of_opcleaving_lift_2cell,, tt)
 abstract
          (cbn ;
           use subtypePath ; [ intro ; apply isapropunit | ] ;
           use disp_nat_trans_eq ;
           intros x xx ;
           cbn ;
           rewrite pr1_transportf ;
           unfold disp_cell_lift_1cell_factor ;
           refine (@disp_nat_trans_transportf
                     _ _
                     _ _
                     (H₁ ∙ F) (H₂ ∙ F)
                     _ _
                     (id2_right (α ▹ F) @ ! id2_left (α ▹ F))
                     (disp_functor_composite
                        (pr11 Lh)
                        (reindex_disp_cat_disp_functor F (pr11 D₂)))
                     (pr1 HH₂)
                     (disp_nat_trans_comp
                        (post_whisker_disp_nat_trans
                           cleaving_of_opcleaving_lift_2cell
                           (reindex_disp_cat_disp_functor F (pr11 D₂)))
                        (pr112 Lh'))
                     x
                     xx
                     @ _) ;
           cbn ;
           unfold cleaving_of_opcleaving_lift_2cell_data ;
           rewrite !mor_disp_transportf_postwhisker ;
           rewrite !transport_f_f ;
           rewrite !assoc_disp_var ;
           rewrite !transport_f_f ;
           etrans ;
           [ do 3 apply maponpaths ;
             apply (z_iso_disp_after_inv_mor
                      (disp_bicat_of_opcleaving_disp_invertible_2cell_pointwise_inv
                         (id2_invertible_2cell (H₂ · F))
                         (pr2 Lh') (pr22 Lh') xx))
           | ] ;
           unfold transportb ;
           rewrite !mor_disp_transportf_prewhisker ;
           rewrite transport_f_f ;
           rewrite id_right_disp ;
           unfold transportb ;
           rewrite mor_disp_transportf_prewhisker ;
           rewrite transport_f_f ;
           apply transportf_set ;
           apply homset_property).
  Defined.
End Lift2CellOpCleaving.
